  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2687307992" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2687307992" />
    <a title="Benjamin Thomas" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4209082-benjamin-thomas"><img alt="Benjamin Thomas" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451660582p2/4209082.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2687307992?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Benjamin Thomas" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Benjamin Thomas" href="/user/show/4209082-benjamin-thomas">Benjamin Thomas</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4209082-benjamin-thomas?shelf=fantasy-epic">fantasy-epic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2687307992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8872128442635218994">The second novel in the Codex Alera series picks up two years after the first one (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29396.Furies_of_Calderon__Codex_Alera___1_' title='Furies of Calderon (Codex Alera, #1) by Jim Butcher' rel='nofollow noopener'>Furies of Calderon</a>) ends. Tavi is now a student at the Academy in the capital city while really being trained as one of the First Lord’s spies. He remains magic-less, unable to call upon the furies but he makes up for that with his intelligence and cleverness. Meanwhile, back in the Calderon Valley, Amara and Bernard team up with Doroga and his clan to face a new threat.<br/><br/>This second book really solidifies the world</span>
  <span id="freeText8872128442635218994" style="display:none">The second novel in the Codex Alera series picks up two years after the first one (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29396.Furies_of_Calderon__Codex_Alera___1_" title="Furies of Calderon (Codex Alera, #1) by Jim Butcher" rel="nofollow noopener">Furies of Calderon</a>) ends. Tavi is now a student at the Academy in the capital city while really being trained as one of the First Lord’s spies. He remains magic-less, unable to call upon the furies but he makes up for that with his intelligence and cleverness. Meanwhile, back in the Calderon Valley, Amara and Bernard team up with Doroga and his clan to face a new threat.<br /><br />This second book really solidifies the world that we got a taste of in book one. Tavi’s presence in the capital city not only leads to all sorts of palace intrigue but also serves as a way for us to learn much more about this world. The main characters are further fleshed out and new, important characters are introduced. I’m really enjoying how the “good” guys and the “bad” guys are becoming grayer in their natures. One’s view of what needs to happen in the world all depends on one’s viewpoint and that drives their actions.<br /><br />Another nice blend of sword-wielding action against formidable foes, heroic moments, romance, and political machinations. This is one of those series of books that I relish living in and don’t have any great desire to rush through to the end. At the same time, I am chomping at the bit to see what comes next so I find more ways to increase my daily reading time. That’s always a sign of a great book or series.<br /><br />On to book three!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8872128442635218994" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7GQmVy0JqrylMo/ltIOBgF8T07CzUho9iYj0R6A7O1Jr1yofs/V8Af5IhcoXEYk5d7TnHLA8x8AJCATfTY+e1w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('w+Pr+73AZpRCmv2fmKn3sdYiYjQmSice0MkUwH5phKpEUOezIzywKRng97A7O/8I/oVWmCUk+uNQSeRYk90hLw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer5670862170406250359">Jim Butcher is the author of the Dresden Files, the Codex Alera, and a new steampunk series, the Cinder Spires. His resume includes a laundry list of skills which were useful a couple of centuries ago, and he plays guitar quite badly. An avid gamer, he plays tabletop games in varying systems, a variety of video games on PC and console, and LARPs whenever he can make time for it. Jim currently resi</span>
  <span id="freeText5670862170406250359" style="display:none">Jim Butcher is the author of the Dresden Files, the Codex Alera, and a new steampunk series, the Cinder Spires. His resume includes a laundry list of skills which were useful a couple of centuries ago, and he plays guitar quite badly. An avid gamer, he plays tabletop games in varying systems, a variety of video games on PC and console, and LARPs whenever he can make time for it. Jim currently resides mostly inside his own head, but his head can generally be found in his home town of Independence, Missouri.<br /><br />Jim goes by the moniker Longshot in a number of online locales. He came by this name in the early 1990′s when he decided he would become a published author. Usually only 3 in 1000 who make such an attempt actually manage to become published; of those, only 1 in 10 make enough money to call it a living. The sale of a second series was the breakthrough that let him beat the long odds against attaining a career as a novelist.<br /><br />All the same, he refuses to change his nickname.<br /></span>
